*TODAY'S QUERY*

*Kindly let me know whether CORONAVIRUS (COVID-19) covered in Health Insurance Policy.*

*YES* CORONAVIRUS (COVID-19) is covered in each and every Health Insurance policy issued in India.

But, if you have taken NEW/FRESH policy then it will be covered from 31st Day of your NEW/FRESH policy also Inception of that diseases also should not falls in first 30 days.

*Example:*

Example : 
Date of Fresh Policy(date of Inception of first/fresh Policy) : 5th March, 2020.

Date of first symptoms of disease : 7th April, 2020

Date of Admission in Hospital: 10th April, 2020

*Whether claim is Paid : This claim will be paid, because Inception of disease is 7th April, 2020 which is after 30 days from taking Health Insurance Policy first time*

This means while counting 30 days time even Inception of disease  will be taken into account. 

*Those who are paying premium from years they don't have to worry about CORONAVIRUS (COVID-19) disease. It's covered in there policy.*

*Kindly don't forget to renew policy before expiry of date.*
